GT Equivalence Verification (I.6.2a)
============================================================
GT: exp(-theta**2/2)/sqrt(2*pi)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: [1, 2, 4, 5, 7]
Matched candidates: ["c0*exp(c1*theta**2)", "c0*exp(c1*theta**2)*cosh(c2*theta)", "c0*exp(c1*theta**2)/cosh(c2*theta)", "c0*exp(c1*theta**2)*cos(c2*theta)", "c0*exp(c1*theta**2)*sin(c2*theta + c3)"]

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth: `exp(-theta**2/2)/sqrt(2*pi)`.

This is a Gaussian function: `c * exp(-theta**2/2)` where `c = 1/sqrt(2*pi)`.

The key structural requirement is that the GT is simply `c0 * exp(c1 * theta**2)` with `c0 = 1/sqrt(2*pi)` and `c1 = -1/2`.

Let me analyze each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*exp(c1*theta**2)`
Set c0 = 1/sqrt(2*pi), c1 = -1/2. This exactly matches GT.
Candidate 1 verdict: [MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `c0*exp(c1*theta**2)*cosh(c2*theta)`
Set c2 = 0, then cosh(0) = 1, giving c0*exp(c1*theta**2). Matches GT.
Candidate 2 verdict: [MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `c0*exp(c1*theta**2) + 1/cosh(c2*theta)`
The 1/cosh term can't be zeroed (setting c2→∞ makes it 0 for theta≠0 but not exactly). We can't set constants to infinity. If c2=0, 1/cosh(0)=1, giving c0*exp(c1*theta**2)+1, which is not the GT. We cannot eliminate the sech term with any finite constant.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `c0*exp(c1*theta**2)/cosh(c2*theta)`
Set c2 = 0, cosh(0) = 1. Matches GT.
Candidate 4 verdict: [MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** `c0*exp(c1*theta**2)*cos(c2*theta)`
Set c2 = 0, cos(0) = 1. Matches GT.
Candidate 5 verdict: [MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** `c0*exp(c1*theta**2)*cos(c2*theta) + 1/cosh(c3*theta)`
Same issue as Candidate 3 - can't eliminate 1/cosh term.
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 7:** `c0*exp(c1*theta**2)*sin(c2*theta + c3)`
Set c2 = 0, c3 = pi/2, then sin(pi/2) = 1. Gives c0*exp(c1*theta**2). Matches GT.
